          <button
            onClick={() => { setAlertaOpen(o=>!o); setAlertaEnviada(false); }}
            style={{ ...btnP({ fontSize:"12px", padding:"8px 16px" }), background:"#FF4B2B", boxShadow:"0 4px 16px rgba(255,75,43,.35)", flexShrink:0 }}
          >
            🚨 Alerta por Robo
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Formulario de alerta — se despliega al clickear el botón */}
      {alertaOpen && (
        <div style={{ background:"rgba(255,75,43,.06)", border:"1px solid rgba(255,75,43,.3)", borderRadius:"14px", padding:"1.5rem", marginBottom:"1.5rem" }} className="pa">
          {alertaEnviada ? (
            <div style={{ textAlign:"center", padding:"1.5rem 0" }}>
              <div style={{ fontSize:"52px", marginBottom:"1rem" }}>🚨</div>
              <div style={{ ...syne, fontSize:"18px", fontWeight:800, color:"#FF4B2B", marginBottom:".5rem" }}>Alerta Activada</div>
              <div style={{ fontSize:"13px", color:MU, marginBottom:".5rem" }}>
                CIT <strong style={{color:TX}}>{form.cit}</strong> bloqueado en la red RODAID.
              </div>
              <div style={{ fontSize:"12px", color:MU, marginBottom:"1.25rem", ...mono }}>
                rodaiEvents.emit('alerta_robo') → 📱 Push · 📧 Email · 📲 SMS
              </div>
              <div style={{ background:"rgba(255,75,43,.1)", borderRadius:"10px", padding:".75rem 1rem", marginBottom:"1.25rem", textAlign:"left", fontSize:"12px" }}>
                <div style={{ color:"#FF4B2B", fontWeight:700, marginBottom:".25rem" }}>Datos registrados</div>
                <div style={{ color:MU }}>🚲 CIT: <span style={{color:TX}}>{form.cit}</span></div>
                <div style={{ color:MU }}>📍 Lugar: <span style={{color:TX}}>{form.lugar}</span></div>
                <div style={{ color:MU }}>🕐 Horario: <span style={{color:TX}}>{form.horario}</span></div>
                {denuncia && <div style={{ color:MU }}>📄 Denuncia PDF: <span style={{color:T}}>{denuncia}</span></div>}
                {fotos.length>0 && <div style={{ color:MU }}>📷 Fotos: <span style={{color:T}}>{fotos.length} cargada(s)</span></div>}
              </div>
              <button onClick={() => { setAlertaOpen(false); setAlertaEnviada(false); setFormAlerta({cit:"",lugar:"",horario:"",descripcion:""}); setFotos([]); setDenuncia(null); }}
                style={btnS()}>Cerrar</button>
            </div>
          ) : (
            <>
              <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:".75rem", marginBottom:"1.5rem" }}>
                <div style={{ width:"36px", height:"36px", borderRadius:"9px", background:"rgba(255,75,43,.15)", border:"1px solid rgba(255,75,43,.3)", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", fontSize:"18px" }}>🚨</div>
                <div>
                  <div style={{ ...syne, fontSize:"15px", fontWeight:800, color:"#FF4B2B" }}>Protocolo de Alerta por Robo</div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize:"11px", color:MU }}>POST /api/seguridad/denunciar · Ley 9556 · BFA</div>
                </div>
              </div>

              <div style={{ display:"grid", gridTemplateColumns:"repeat(auto-fit,minmax(240px,1fr))", gap:"1rem", marginBottom:"1rem" }}>
                {/* CIT de la Bicicleta */}
                <div>
                  <label style={{ fontSize:"11px", fontWeight:700, color:"#FF4B2B", display:"block", marginBottom:".4rem", letterSpacing:".5px" }}>CIT DE LA BICICLETA *</label>
                  <select value={form.cit} onChange={e=>setField("cit",e.target.value)} style={{ ...inputStyle }}>
                    <option value="">Seleccioná el CIT</option>
                    {usuario.bicicletas.map(b => (
                      <option key={b.id} value={b.certId}>#{b.certId} — {b.m} ({b.sn})</option>
                    ))}
                  </select>
                </div>
                {/* Lugar de Robo */}
                <div>
                  <label style={{ fontSize:"11px", fontWeight:700, color:"#FF4B2B", display:"block", marginBottom:".4rem", letterSpacing:".5px" }}>LUGAR DEL ROBO *</label>
                  <input type="text" value={form.lugar} onChange={e=>setField("lugar",e.target.value)}
                    placeholder="Ej: Av. San Martín 450, San Martín, Mendoza"
                    style={inputStyle} onFocus={e=>e.target.style.borderColor="#FF4B2B"} onBlur={e=>e.target.style.borderColor="rgba(255,75,43,.25)"} />
                </div>
                {/* Horario */}
                <div>
                  <label style={{ fontSize:"11px", fontWeight:700, color:"#FF4B2B", display:"block", marginBottom:".4rem", letterSpacing:".5px" }}>HORARIO *</label>
                  <input type="datetime-local" value={form.horario} onChange={e=>setField("horario",e.target.value)}
                    style={{ ...inputStyle, colorScheme:"dark" }} />
                </div>
                {/* Descripción */}
                <div>
                  <label style={{ fontSize:"11px", fontWeight:700, color:MU, display:"block", marginBottom:".4rem", letterSpacing:".5px" }}>DESCRIPCIÓN</label>
                  <input type="text" value={form.descripcion} onChange={e=>setField("descripcion",e.target.value)}
                    placeholder="Color, características especiales, testigos..."
                    style={inputStyle} onFocus={e=>e.target.style.borderColor="#FF4B2B"} onBlur={e=>e.target.style.borderColor="rgba(255,75,43,.25)"} />
                </div>
              </div>

              <div style={{ display:"grid", gridTemplateColumns:"repeat(auto-fit,minmax(240px,1fr))", gap:"1rem", marginBottom:"1.5rem" }}>
                {/* Denuncia Policial PDF */}
                <div>
                  <label style={{ fontSize:"11px", fontWeight:700, color:MU, display:"block", marginBottom:".4rem", letterSpacing:".5px" }}>📄 DENUNCIA POLICIAL (PDF)</label>
                  <button onClick={() => setDenuncia("denuncia_policial_"+Date.now()+".pdf")}
                    style={{ width:"100%", padding:"20px 14px", borderRadius:"9px", border:"2px dashed rgba(255,75,43,.3)", background: denuncia?"rgba(43,188,184,.06)":"rgba(255,255,255,.02)", cursor:"pointer", fontSize:"12px", color: denuncia?T:MU, transition:"all .2s", textAlign:"center" }}
                    onMouseEnter={e=>e.currentTarget.style.borderColor="#FF4B2B"} onMouseLeave={e=>e.currentTarget.style.borderColor="rgba(255,75,43,.3)"}>
                    {denuncia ? <><div style={{fontSize:"20px",marginBottom:"4px"}}>✅</div>{denuncia}</> : <><div style={{fontSize:"24px",marginBottom:"4px"}}>📎</div>Cargar PDF de denuncia</>}
                  </button>
                </div>

                {/* Fotos de la Unidad */}
                <div>
                  <label style={{ fontSize:"11px", fontWeight:700, color:MU, display:"block", marginBottom:".4rem", letterSpacing:".5px" }}>📷 FOTOS DE LA UNIDAD ROBADA</label>
                  <button onClick={() => setFotos(f => [...f, `foto_bici_${f.length+1}_${Date.now()}.jpg`])}
                    style={{ width:"100%", padding:"20px 14px", borderRadius:"9px", border:"2px dashed rgba(255,75,43,.3)", background: fotos.length?"rgba(43,188,184,.06)":"rgba(255,255,255,.02)", cursor:"pointer", fontSize:"12px", color: fotos.length?T:MU, transition:"all .2s", textAlign:"center" }}
                    onMouseEnter={e=>e.currentTarget.style.borderColor="#FF4B2B"} onMouseLeave={e=>e.currentTarget.style.borderColor="rgba(255,75,43,.3)"}>
                    <div style={{fontSize:"24px",marginBottom:"4px"}}>📷</div>
                    {fotos.length ? `${fotos.length} foto(s) cargada(s) · + Agregar` : "Cargar fotos de la bici"}
                  </button>
                  {fotos.length > 0 && (
                    <div style={{ display:"flex", flexWrap:"wrap", gap:".35rem", marginTop:".5rem" }}>
                      {fotos.map((f,i) => <span key={i} style={{ fontSize:"10px", color:T, background:"rgba(43,188,184,.1)", padding:"2px 8px", borderRadius:"6px", border:"1px solid rgba(43,188,184,.25)" }}>{f}</span>)}
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* Aviso legal */}
              <div style={{ fontSize:"11px", color:MU, background:"rgba(255,255,255,.03)", borderRadius:"8px", padding:".6rem 1rem", marginBottom:"1.25rem", lineHeight:1.6 }}>
                ⚠️ Esta acción <strong style={{color:"#FF4B2B"}}>bloqueará cualquier transferencia en Blockchain</strong> del rodado seleccionado y disparará una alerta inmediata a la red de talleres Aliados de la Zona Este.
              </div>

              <button onClick={activarAlerta} disabled={enviando || !form.cit || !form.lugar || !form.horario}
                style={{ ...btnP({ width:"100%", fontSize:"14px", padding:"13px" }), background: (enviando||!form.cit||!form.lugar||!form.horario)?"#8B3020":"#FF4B2B", boxShadow:"0 4px 20px rgba(255,75,43,.3)", opacity:(enviando||!form.cit||!form.lugar||!form.horario)?.6:1 }}>
                {enviando ? "ACTIVANDO PROTOCOLO..." : "🚨 ACTIVAR ALERTA DE ROBO"}
              </button>
            </>
          )}
        </div>
      )}

      {usuario.plan==="Premium" ? <PlantillaPremium usuario={usuario} showToast={showToast} /> : <PlantillaEstandar usuario={usuario} showToast={showToast} />}
    </div>
  );
}

// ─── MAPA MOVILIDAD ─────────────────────────────────────
// asignarAsistencia() + procesarRutaLimpia() + MapaMovilidad
function PageMovilidad({ nav, showToast, emitEvent }) {
  const [asignando, setAsignando] = useState(false);
  const [asistencia, setAsistencia] = useState(null);
  const [ruta, setRuta] = useState([]);
  const userLocation = { lat:-33.0819, lng:-68.4709 }; // San Martín centro

  // Talleres Aliados Zona Este — db.Talleres.find({ activo:true, zona:"Zona Este" })
  const talleres = [
    { nombre:"Taller Central San Martín", lat:-33.0819, lng:-68.4709, zona:"San Martín", dist:"0.4 km", tiempo:"3 mins" },
    { nombre:"Ciclos Junín Norte",         lat:-33.1012, lng:-68.5431, zona:"Junín",      dist:"12 km",  tiempo:"18 mins" },
    { nombre:"Biciclería Rivadavia",       lat:-33.1887, lng:-68.4612, zona:"Rivadavia",  dist:"18 km",  tiempo:"26 mins" },
    { nombre:"Moto & Ciclo San Martín",    lat:-33.0750, lng:-68.4620, zona:"San Martín", dist:"1.2 km", tiempo:"8 mins"  },
  ];
  const alertaZonas = [{ lat:-33.090, lng:-68.480, info:"Zona de Alerta Reciente" }];

  // asignarAsistencia() — selecciona taller más cercano por duration
  const asignarAsistencia = async () => {
    setAsignando(true);
    setAsistencia(null);
    showToast("Consultando Google Maps Distance Matrix...", "info");
    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 1800));
    // mode: 'bicycling' — mejor taller por tiempo
    const mejor = talleres.reduce((min, t) => parseInt(t.tiempo)<parseInt(min.tiempo)?t:min);
    setAsistencia(mejor);
    emitEvent("cit_emitido", `Asistencia asignada: ${mejor.nombre} · ETA ${mejor.tiempo}`);
    showToast(`Taller asignado: ${mejor.nombre} · ${mejor.tiempo}`, "success");
    setAsignando(false);
  };

  // procesarRutaLimpia() — snapToRoads interpolation
  const procesarRuta = () => {
    const puntos = [
      { lat:-33.0819, lng:-68.4709 },{ lat:-33.0830, lng:-68.4720 },
      { lat:-33.0845, lng:-68.4735 },{ lat:-33.0860, lng:-68.4748 },
    ];
    setRuta(puntos);
    showToast("procesarRutaLimpia() — snapToRoads ✓ interpolate:true", "success");
  };

  // SVG map helper — convert lat/lng to pixel
  const toXY = (lat, lng) => ({
    x: ((lng - (-68.56)) / ((-68.43) - (-68.56))) * 520 + 20,
    y: ((lat - (-33.21)) / ((-33.06) - (-33.21))) * 360 + 20,
  });

  return (
    <div>
      <div style={{ background:"rgba(0,0,0,.15)", borderBottom:`1px solid ${BO}`, padding:"3rem 2rem" }}>
        <div style={wrap}>
          <div style={lbl()}>Google Maps Integration</div>
          <h1 style={{ ...syne, fontSize:"clamp(1.8rem,3vw,2.5rem)", fontWeight:800, letterSpacing:"-1px", marginBottom:".75rem" }}>
            Mapa de <span style={{color:T}}>Movilidad</span>
          </h1>
          <p style={{ color:MU, maxWidth:"540px", lineHeight:1.7 }}>
            Red de talleres Aliados con asignación automática por distancia. Integración con Distance Matrix API en modo <code style={{color:T}}>bicycling</code>.
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
      <section style={sec()}>
        <div style={wrap}>
          <div style={{ display:"grid", gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr", gap:"1.5rem", alignItems:"start" }}>
            {/* SVG Map — MapaMovilidad */}
            <div style={{ ...card({ padding:0, overflow:"hidden" }) }}>
              <div style={{ padding:".75rem 1rem", borderBottom:`1px solid ${BO}`, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:".5rem" }}>
                <span style={{ width:"8px", height:"8px", borderRadius:"50%", background:T, display:"inline-block", animation:"pulse 2s infinite" }} />
                <span style={{ fontSize:"12px", fontWeight:600, color:T }}>MapaMovilidad · Zona Este Mendoza</span>
                <span style={{ marginLeft:"auto", fontSize:"10px", color:MU, ...mono }}>mode: 'bicycling'</span>
              </div>
              <svg viewBox="0 0 560 400" style={{ width:"100%", background:"#0F1E2E" }}>
                {/* Grid lines */}
                {[0,1,2,3].map(i=><line key={i} x1={i*140+20} y1="20" x2={i*140+20} y2="380" stroke="rgba(255,255,255,.04)" strokeWidth="1"/>)}
                {[0,1,2,3].map(i=><line key={i} x1="20" y1={i*120+20} x2="540" y2={i*120+20} stroke="rgba(255,255,255,.04)" strokeWidth="1"/>)}
                {/* Zone labels */}
                <text x="80" y="40" fill="rgba(255,255,255,.2)" fontSize="10" fontFamily="monospace">San Martín</text>
                <text x="280" y="200" fill="rgba(255,255,255,.2)" fontSize="10" fontFamily="monospace">Junín</text>
                <text x="80" y="340" fill="rgba(255,255,255,.2)" fontSize="10" fontFamily="monospace">Rivadavia</text>
                {/* Ruta limpia — procesarRutaLimpia() snapToRoads */}
                {ruta.length > 1 && (
                  <polyline points={ruta.map(p=>`${toXY(p.lat,p.lng).x},${toXY(p.lat,p.lng).y}`).join(" ")}
                    fill="none" stroke={O} strokeWidth="3" strokeDasharray="6,3" strokeLinecap="round"/>
                )}
                {/* Zona alerta */}
                {alertaZonas.map((z,i)=>{const {x,y}=toXY(z.lat,z.lng);return(
                  <g key={i}>
                    <circle cx={x} cy={y} r="20" fill="rgba(231,76,60,.12)" stroke="rgba(231,76,60,.3)" strokeWidth="1"/>
                    <text x={x} y={y+4} textAnchor="middle" fill="#e74c3c" fontSize="11">⚠️</text>
                  </g>
                )})}
                {/* User location */}
                {(()=>{const {x,y}=toXY(userLocation.lat,userLocation.lng);return(
                  <g>
                    <circle cx={x} cy={y} r="14" fill="rgba(244,123,32,.15)" stroke={O} strokeWidth="1.5"/>
                    <circle cx={x} cy={y} r="5" fill={O}/>
                    <text x={x} y={y-18} textAnchor="middle" fill={O} fontSize="9" fontFamily="monospace">Tu ubicación</text>
                  </g>
                )})()}
                {/* Talleres */}
                {talleres.map((t,i)=>{const {x,y}=toXY(t.lat,t.lng);const isBest=asistencia?.nombre===t.nombre;return(
                  <g key={i}>
                    <circle cx={x} cy={y} r={isBest?12:8} fill={isBest?"rgba(43,188,184,.25)":"rgba(255,255,255,.08)"} stroke={isBest?T:"rgba(255,255,255,.2)"} strokeWidth={isBest?2:1}/>
                    <text x={x} y={y+4} textAnchor="middle" fill={isBest?T:"rgba(255,255,255,.6)"} fontSize="9">🔧</text>
                    <text x={x} y={y-14} textAnchor="middle" fill={isBest?T:"rgba(255,255,255,.4)"} fontSize="8" fontFamily="monospace">{t.zona}</text>
                    {isBest && <circle cx={x} cy={y} r="20" fill="none" stroke={T} strokeWidth="1" strokeDasharray="4,2" opacity=".6"/>}
                  </g>
                )})}
              </svg>
            </div>

            {/* Controls panel */}
            <div style={{ display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", gap:"1rem" }}>
              {/* asignarAsistencia() */}
              <div style={card()}>
                <div style={{ ...syne, fontSize:"14px", fontWeight:700, marginBottom:".5rem" }}>asignarAsistencia()</div>
                <p style={{ fontSize:"12px", color:MU, marginBottom:"1rem", lineHeight:1.6 }}>
                  Distance Matrix API · mode: <code style={{color:T}}>'bicycling'</code> · selecciona el taller más cercano por <code style={{color:T}}>duration.value</code>
                </p>
                <button onClick={asignarAsistencia} disabled={asignando} style={{ ...btnP({ width:"100%", fontSize:"13px", opacity:asignando?.6:1 }) }}>
                  {asignando ? "Calculando ruta..." : "🔧 Asignar Asistencia"}
                </button>
                {asistencia && (
                  <div style={{ marginTop:"1rem", background:"rgba(43,188,184,.08)", border:"1px solid rgba(43,188,184,.2)", borderRadius:"10px", padding:".85rem" }} className="pa">
                    <div style={{ fontSize:"13px", fontWeight:700, color:T, marginBottom:".4rem" }}>{asistencia.nombre}</div>
                    {[["zona",asistencia.zona],["distancia",asistencia.dist],["tiempoEstimado",asistencia.tiempo]].map(([l,v],i)=>(
                      <div key={i} style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", fontSize:"12px", padding:".2rem 0" }}>
                        <span style={{color:MU,...mono}}>{l}:</span>
                        <span style={{fontWeight:600,color:T}}>{v}</span>
                      </div>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>

              {/* procesarRutaLimpia() */}
              <div style={card()}>
                <div style={{ ...syne, fontSize:"14px", fontWeight:700, marginBottom:".5rem" }}>procesarRutaLimpia()</div>
                <p style={{ fontSize:"12px", color:MU, marginBottom:"1rem", lineHeight:1.6 }}>
                  snapToRoads API · <code style={{color:O}}>interpolate: true</code> · ajusta puntos GPS al trazado vial real
                </p>
                <button onClick={procesarRuta} style={{ ...btnS({ width:"100%", fontSize:"13px" }) }}>
                  📍 Simular GPS Track
                </button>
                {ruta.length > 0 && (
                  <div style={{ marginTop:".75rem", background:"rgba(244,123,32,.06)", border:"1px solid rgba(244,123,32,.2)", borderRadius:"8px", padding:".6rem .85rem" }} className="pa">
                    <div style={{ fontSize:"10px", color:MU, ...mono }}>snappedPoints ({ruta.length})</div>
                    {ruta.map((p,i)=><div key={i} style={{ fontSize:"10px", color:O, ...mono }}>→ lat:{p.lat.toFixed(4)}, lng:{p.lng.toFixed(4)}</div>)}
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>

              {/* Talleres list */}
              <div style={card()}>
                <div style={{ ...lbl(T), marginBottom:".75rem" }}>db.Talleres · Zona Este</div>
                {talleres.map((t,i)=>(
                  <div key={i} style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"center", padding:".4rem 0", borderBottom:i<3?`1px solid ${BO}`:"none", fontSize:"12px" }}>
                    <span style={{color:asistencia?.nombre===t.nombre?T:TX}}>🔧 {t.nombre}</span>
                    <span style={{color:MU,...mono}}>{t.tiempo}</span>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </section>

      {/* ExploradorRutasWikiloc — Wikiloc API */}
      <ExploradorRutasWikiloc showToast={showToast} />

      {/* PageAdminMovilidad — Smart City */}
      <PageAdminMovilidad showToast={showToast} emitEvent={emitEvent} />
    </div>
  );
}

// ─── PAGE VERIFICADOR PÚBLICO ────────────────────────────
function PageVerificador({ nav, showToast, emitEvent }) {
  const [query, setQuery] = useState("");
  const [status, setStatus] = useState(null); // null | "clean" | "stolen" | "notfound"
  const [result, setResult] = useState(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [verifyStep, setVerifyStep] = useState(0); // 0=idle 1=db 2=bfa 3=compare
  const [apiResponse, setApiResponse] = useState(null); // { identidad, propietario, verificado_blockchain, alerta }

  // Mock database
  const db = [
    { sn:"SN-R84MK-TMIA-MZA",  hash:"0x14b28607f44e", model:"Trek Marlin 7",           owner:"F******* D* G**",   date:"11/05/2026", loc:"San Martín, Mendoza",  state:"clean"  },
    { sn:"SN-9923410056-MZA",   hash:"f47b203660",    model:"Specialized Rockhopper 29", owner:"M*** V**",          date:"10/05/2026", loc:"Junín, Mendoza",        state:"clean"  },
    { sn:"SN-GTC2023-RTA-MZA",  hash:"a9f3c14v",      model:"Giant TCR Advanced",        owner:"C*** R***",         date:"08/05/2026", loc:"Rivadavia, Mendoza",    state:"clean"  },
    { sn:"SN-CGF2024-RTA-MZA",  hash:"b2e4d55p",      model:"Canyon Grail CF",           owner:"L*** M***",         date:"05/05/2026", loc:"San Martín, Mendoza",  state:"stolen" },
    { sn:"SN-CA2023-MTB-MZA",   hash:"c3f5e66q",      model:"Cube Attention",            owner:"J*** P***",         date:"01/04/2026", loc:"Rivadavia, Mendoza",    state:"clean"  },
  ];

  const consultarUnidad = () => {
    // Reset
    setStatus(null); setResult(null); setApiResponse(null); setVerifyStep(0);

    const q = query.trim().toUpperCase();
    if (q === "") { showToast("Ingresá un número de serie", "info"); return; }

    setLoading(true);
    showToast("Consultando base de datos y Blockchain...", "success");

    // Paso 1: Bicicleta.findOne({ serial_cuadro: serial })
    setVerifyStep(1);
    setTimeout(() => {
      const found = q.includes("ROBO") || q === "123"
        ? db.find(b => b.state === "stolen") || db[3]
        : db.find(b => b.sn.toUpperCase().includes(q) || b.hash.toUpperCase().includes(q))
          || (q.length > 5 ? { sn:q, model:"Unidad Detectada: "+q, owner:"P******* D***", date:new Date().toLocaleDateString("es-AR"), loc:"Mendoza, Argentina", hash:"0x"+q.toLowerCase().slice(0,8)+"...", state:"clean" } : null);

      if (!found) {
        setLoading(false); setVerifyStep(0);
        setStatus("notfound");
        showToast("Bicicleta no registrada", "info");
        return;
      }

      // Paso 2: rodaidContract.getHash(serial)
      setVerifyStep(2);
      setTimeout(() => {
        // Paso 3: Comparar integridad (hashActual === hashOriginal)
        setVerifyStep(3);
        setTimeout(() => {
          setLoading(false); setVerifyStep(0);
          const isStolenQuery = q.includes("ROBO") || q === "123";
          const verificado_blockchain = !isStolenQuery;
          const alerta = verificado_blockchain ? "ORIGINAL" : "RODADO CON DENUNCIA DE ROBO";
          const httpStatus = isStolenQuery ? 403 : 200;
          setApiResponse({ identidad: found.sn, propietario: found.owner, verificado_blockchain, alerta, status: httpStatus });
          setResult(found);
          setStatus(isStolenQuery ? "stolen" : found.state);
          if (isStolenQuery) {
            // rodaiEvents.emit('alerta_robo', { userId, email, telefono, mensaje })
            emitEvent("alerta_robo",
              `¡ALERTA! Alguien intentó verificar ${found.sn} desde San Martín, Mendoza.`
            );
            showToast("⚠️ 403 · RODADO CON DENUNCIA DE ROBO", "info");
          } else {
            showToast("200 · Integridad verificada — ORIGINAL ✓", "success");
          }
        if (!verificado_blockchain) emitEvent && emitEvent("alerta_robo", `Alerta SECURITY: ${found.model} · ${found.sn}`);
        }, 500);
      }, 700);
    }, 800);
  };

  const examples = ["SN-R84MK-TMIA-MZA","SN-CGF2024-RTA-MZA","SN-9923410056-MZA"];

  return (
    <div>
      {/* Hero */}
      <div style={{ position:"relative", background:"rgba(0,0,0,.15)", borderBottom:`1px solid ${BO}`, padding:"4rem 2rem 3rem", textAlign:"center" }}>
        <div style={{ position:"absolute", inset:0, background:"radial-gradient(ellipse 50% 60% at 50% 0%,rgba(43,188,184,.08) 0%,transparent 70%)" }} />
        <div style={{ position:"relative", zIndex:2 }}>
          <div style={lbl()}>Protocolo de Seguridad</div>
          <h1 style={{ ...syne, fontSize:"clamp(1.9rem,4vw,2.8rem)", fontWeight:800, letterSpacing:"-1px", marginBottom:".75rem" }}>
            Consultá el <span style={{ color:T }}>Estado Legal</span>
          </h1>
          <p style={{ color:MU, fontSize:"15px", maxWidth:"520px", margin:"0 auto 2rem", lineHeight:1.75 }}>
            Verificá instantáneamente si una unidad posee denuncia por robo o si su certificado blockchain es válido.
          </p>

          {/* Search box */}
          <div className="chain-bar-live" style={{ alignItems:"center", boxShadow:"0 8px 40px rgba(0,0,0,.3)", paddingLeft:"16px" }}>
            <span style={{ fontSize:"18px", flexShrink:0 }}>🔍</span>
            <input
              value={query}
              onChange={e => setQuery(e.target.value)}
              onKeyDown={e => e.key === "Enter" && consultarUnidad()}
              placeholder="Ingresá N° de Cuadro o Hash RODAID..."
              style={{ flex:1, background:"transparent", border:"none", outline:"none", color:TX, fontSize:"14px", fontFamily:"'Manrope',sans-serif" }}
            />
            <button
              onClick={consultarUnidad}
              disabled={loading}
              style={{ ...btnP({ padding:"10px 22px", fontSize:"13px", opacity:loading?.7:1, flexShrink:0 }) }}>
              {loading ? "Verificando..." : "Verificar Unidad"}
            </button>
          </div>

          {/* Example queries */}
          <div style={{ marginTop:"1rem", display:"flex", gap:".5rem", justifyContent:"center", flexWrap:"wrap" }}>
            <span style={{ fontSize:"12px", color:MU }}>Ejemplos:</span>
            {examples.map(ex => (
              <button key={ex} onClick={() => setQuery(ex)} style={{ background:"rgba(255,255,255,.05)", border:`1px solid ${BO}`, color:MU, fontSize:"11px", padding:"3px 10px", borderRadius:"20px", cursor:"pointer", ...mono, transition:"all .2s" }}
                onMouseEnter={e => { e.currentTarget.style.borderColor=T; e.currentTarget.style.color=T; }}
                onMouseLeave={e => { e.currentTarget.style.borderColor=BO; e.currentTarget.style.color=MU; }}>
                {ex}
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <section style={sec()}>
        <div style={{ maxWidth:"680px", margin:"0 auto" }}>

          {/* Loading */}
          {loading && (
            <div style={{ background:"rgba(0,0,0,.15)", borderRadius:"14px", padding:"1.5rem", border:`1px solid ${BO}` }} className="pa">
              <div style={{ ...lbl(T), marginBottom:"1rem" }}>GET /api/verificar/{query} — Express Route</div>
              {[
                { step:1, label:"Bicicleta.findOne({ serial_cuadro })", desc:"Paso 1 · Consulta en base de datos local", icon:"🗄️" },
                { step:2, label:"rodaidContract.getHash(serial)", desc:"Paso 2 · Recuperar hash original de BFA", icon:"⛓️" },
                { step:3, label:"sha256(dataActual) === hashOriginal", desc:"Paso 3 · Comparación de integridad", icon:"🔐" },
              ].map(s => (
                <div key={s.step} style={{ display:"flex", gap:".75rem", alignItems:"center", padding:".5rem 0", opacity: verifyStep >= s.step ? 1 : .25, transition:"opacity .35s" }}>
                  <div style={{ width:"32px", height:"32px", borderRadius:"8px", background: verifyStep > s.step ? "rgba(43,188,184,.2)" : verifyStep === s.step ? "rgba(244,123,32,.15)" : CB, flexShrink:0, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", fontSize:"15px", border: verifyStep > s.step ? `1px solid rgba(43,188,184,.4)` : verifyStep === s.step ? `1px solid rgba(244,123,32,.4)` : `1px solid ${BO}`, transition:"all .35s" }}>
                    {verifyStep > s.step ? "✓" : s.icon}
                  </div>
                  <div style={{ flex:1 }}>
                    <div style={{ ...mono, fontSize:"12px", color: verifyStep > s.step ? T : verifyStep === s.step ? O : MU, transition:"color .35s" }}>{s.label}</div>
                    <div style={{ fontSize:"10px", color:MU }}>{s.desc}</div>
                  </div>
                  {verifyStep === s.step && <div style={{ width:"16px", height:"16px", borderRadius:"50%", border:`2px solid ${O}`, borderTop:"2px solid transparent", animation:"spin 1s linear infinite", flexShrink:0 }} />}
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}

          {/* ESTADO: LIMPIO */}
          {status === "clean" && result && (
            <div style={{ border:"1px solid rgba(43,188,184,.35)", borderRadius:"16px", overflow:"hidden", background:"rgba(43,188,184,.04)" }} className="pa">
              <div style={{ background:"rgba(43,188,184,.12)", borderBottom:`1px solid rgba(43,188,184,.2)`, padding:"1rem 1.5rem", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:"10px" }}>
                <span style={{ fontSize:"20px" }}>✅</span>
                <div style={{ ...syne, fontSize:"14px", fontWeight:800, color:T, letterSpacing:"1px" }}>ESTADO: LIMPIO</div>
                <div style={{ marginLeft:"auto", display:"flex", gap:".5rem", flexWrap:"wrap" }}>
                  <div style={{ fontSize:"11px", fontWeight:700, padding:"4px 12px", borderRadius:"20px", background:"rgba(43,188,184,.2)", color:T, border:`1px solid rgba(43,188,184,.3)` }}>CIT Verificado · BFA</div>
                  {apiResponse && <div style={{ fontSize:"11px", fontWeight:700, padding:"4px 12px", borderRadius:"20px", background:"rgba(43,188,184,.15)", color:T, border:`1px solid rgba(43,188,184,.25)` }}>alerta: "{apiResponse.alerta}"</div>}
                </div>
              </div>
              <div style={{ padding:"1.5rem" }}>
                <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"flex-start", flexWrap:"wrap", gap:"1rem", marginBottom:"1.25rem" }}>
                  <div>
                    <h3 style={{ ...syne, fontSize:"1.4rem", fontWeight:800, marginBottom:".25rem" }}>{result.model}</h3>
                    <p style={{ color:MU, fontSize:"13px" }}>Propiedad de: <strong style={{color:TX}}>{result.owner}</strong></p>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div style={{ width:"100%", height:"1px", background:BO, margin:"1rem 0" }} />
                <div style={{ display:"grid", gridTemplateColumns:"repeat(auto-fit,minmax(140px,1fr))", gap:"1rem" }}>
                  {[
                    {l:"N° DE CUADRO", v:result.sn, mono:true},
                    {l:"ÚLTIMO REGISTRO", v:result.date},
                    {l:"ORIGEN", v:result.loc},
                    {l:"RED BLOCKCHAIN", v:"Mendoza-Mainnet · BFA"},
                    ...(apiResponse ? [{l:"VERIFICADO BLOCKCHAIN", v:apiResponse.verificado_blockchain ? "✓ true" : "✗ false", c:apiResponse.verificado_blockchain?T:"#FF6B6B"}] : []),
                  ].map((f,i) => (
                    <div key={i}>
                      <div style={{ fontSize:"10px", fontWeight:700, letterSpacing:"1.5px", color:MU, marginBottom:".3rem" }}>{f.l}</div>
                      <div style={{ fontSize:"13px", fontWeight:600, fontFamily:f.mono?"monospace":"inherit" }}>{f.v}</div>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
                {apiResponse && (
                <div style={{ display:"inline-flex", alignItems:"center", gap:".5rem", marginBottom:".75rem", fontSize:"11px", ...mono }}>
                  <span style={{ padding:"3px 10px", borderRadius:"6px", background:"rgba(43,188,184,.15)", color:T, fontWeight:700 }}>res.status({apiResponse.status||200})</span>
                  <span style={{ color:MU }}>alerta: "{apiResponse.alerta}"</span>
                </div>
              )}
              <div style={{ marginTop:"1.25rem", background:"rgba(0,0,0,.2)", borderRadius:"10px", padding:".75rem 1rem", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:".75rem" }}>
                  <span style={{ fontSize:"14px" }}>⛓️</span>
                  <div>
                    <div style={{ fontSize:"10px", color:MU, marginBottom:"2px", letterSpacing:"1px" }}>BLOCKCHAIN HASH</div>
                    <code style={{ fontSize:"12px", color:T, ...mono }}>{result.hash}</code>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* ESTADO: DENUNCIA */}
          {status === "stolen" && result && (
            <div style={{ border:"1px solid rgba(231,76,60,.4)", borderRadius:"16px", overflow:"hidden", background:"rgba(231,76,60,.06)" }} className="pa">
              <div style={{ background:"rgba(231,76,60,.15)", borderBottom:"1px solid rgba(231,76,60,.3)", padding:"1rem 1.5rem", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:"10px" }}>
                <span style={{ fontSize:"20px" }}>⚠️</span>
                <div style={{ ...syne, fontSize:"14px", fontWeight:800, color:"#e74c3c", letterSpacing:"1px" }}>RODADO CON DENUNCIA DE ROBO</div>
                <div style={{ marginLeft:"auto", fontSize:"11px", fontWeight:700, padding:"3px 10px", borderRadius:"8px", background:"rgba(231,76,60,.2)", color:"#e74c3c", ...mono }}>res.status(403)</div>
              </div>
              <div style={{ padding:"1.5rem", textAlign:"center" }}>
                <div style={{ fontSize:"48px", marginBottom:"1rem" }}>🚨</div>
                <h3 style={{ ...syne, fontSize:"1.3rem", fontWeight:800, color:"#e74c3c", marginBottom:".75rem" }}>
                  Esta bicicleta ha sido reportada como sustraída
                </h3>
                <p style={{ color:MU, fontSize:"14px", lineHeight:1.75, marginBottom:"1rem" }}>
                  <strong style={{color:TX}}>{result.model}</strong> fue reportada el <strong style={{color:TX}}>10/05/2026</strong>.<br/>
                  Si tenés esta bicicleta en tu poder, contactá a las autoridades.
                </p>
                {/* rodaiEvents.emit('alerta_robo') — fired automatically */}
                <div style={{ background:"rgba(231,76,60,.08)", border:"1px solid rgba(231,76,60,.25)", borderRadius:"10px", padding:".75rem 1rem", marginBottom:"1rem", textAlign:"left", fontSize:"12px" }}>
                  <div style={{ ...mono, color:"#e74c3c", marginBottom:".3rem", fontWeight:700 }}>rodaiEvents.emit('alerta_robo')</div>
                  <div style={{ color:MU }}>📱 Push · 📧 Email · 📲 SMS → propietario notificado</div>
                  <div style={{ color:MU, ...mono, fontSize:"11px", marginTop:".25rem" }}>mensaje: "¡ALERTA! Alguien intentó verificar {result.sn} desde San Martín, Mendoza."</div>
                </div>
                <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:"10px", justifyContent:"center", flexWrap:"wrap" }}>
                  <button style={{ background:"rgba(231,76,60,.15)", border:"1px solid rgba(231,76,60,.4)", color:"#e74c3c", padding:"10px 22px", borderRadius:"10px", fontWeight:600, fontSize:"13px", cursor:"pointer" }}>
                    Contactar al Dueño Original
                  </button>
                  <button style={{ background:"rgba(0,0,0,.2)", border:`1px solid ${BO}`, color:MU, padding:"10px 22px", borderRadius:"10px", fontWeight:600, fontSize:"13px", cursor:"pointer" }}>
                    Reportar a Autoridades
                  </button>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* NO ENCONTRADO */}
          {status === "notfound" && (
            <div style={{ ...card({ textAlign:"center", padding:"2.5rem" }) }} className="pa">
              <div style={{ fontSize:"40px", marginBottom:"1rem" }}>🔎</div>
              <h3 style={{ ...syne, fontSize:"1.2rem", fontWeight:800, marginBottom:".5rem" }}>Unidad no encontrada</h3>
              <p style={{ color:MU, fontSize:"14px", lineHeight:1.75, marginBottom:"1.25rem" }}>
                El N° de cuadro o hash ingresado no figura en el registro RODAID. Puede que la bicicleta no esté certificada aún.
              </p>
              <button onClick={() => nav("registro-bici")} style={btnP()}>Certificar esta bicicleta</button>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* Info cards — visible when no search done */}
          {!status && !loading && (
            <div style={{ display:"grid", gridTemplateColumns:"repeat(auto-fit,minmax(200px,1fr))", gap:"1rem" }} className="pa">
              {[
                { icon:"🛡️", t:"Verificación inmutable", d:"El resultado se obtiene directamente desde la Blockchain Federal Argentina, no puede ser alterado." },
                { icon:"🔒", t:"Privacidad protegida", d:"Los datos del propietario están parcialmente anonimizados. Solo se muestra lo necesario para verificar." },
                { icon:"⚡", t:"Respuesta en segundos", d:"Consulta instantánea al nodo BFA de Mendoza. Sin intermediarios, sin demoras." },
              ].map((c,i) => (
                <div key={i} style={card()}>
                  <div style={{ fontSize:"28px", marginBottom:".75rem" }}>{c.icon}</div>
                  <h4 style={{ ...syne, fontSize:"14px", fontWeight:700, marginBottom:".4rem" }}>{c.t}</h4>
                  <p style={{ fontSize:"12px", color:MU, lineHeight:1.6 }}>{c.d}</p>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      </section>
    </div>
  );
}

// ─── PAGE REGISTRO BICI ──────────────────────────────────
function PageRegistroBici({ nav, showToast, emitEvent }) {
  const [step, setStep] = useState(1);
  const [form, setForm] = useState({ marca:"", modelo:"", serie:"" });
  const [uploads, setUploads] = useState({ lateral:false, cuadro:false, factura:false });
  const [generating, setGenerating] = useState(false);
  const [bfaStep, setBfaStep] = useState(0);
  const [showPDF, setShowPDF] = useState(false);
  const [done, setDone] = useState(false);
  const [hashVal, setHashVal] = useState("");
  const [txHash, setTxHash] = useState("");
  const [idRodaid, setIdRodaid] = useState("");
  // generarNFTRodaid() outputs
  const [ipfsHash, setIpfsHash] = useState("");
  const [tokenId, setTokenId] = useState("");
  const [openseaUrl, setOpenseaUrl] = useState("");
  // Joi schema — puntos_tecnicos + resultado_final
  const [puntos, setPuntos] = useState({
    estructura:false, direccion:false, ergonomia:false,
    transmision:false, frenado:false, ruedas:false,
    identidad:false, conservacion:false, mantenimiento:false, inventario:false,
  });
  const togglePunto = (k) => setPuntos(p => ({ ...p, [k]: !p[k] }));
  const puntosOk = Object.values(puntos).filter(Boolean).length;
  const resultado_final = puntosOk >= 8 ? "aprobado" : puntosOk >= 5 ? "observado" : "rechazado";
  const rfColor = resultado_final === "aprobado" ? T : resultado_final === "observado" ? O : "#FF6B6B";

  const update = (k, v) => setForm(f => ({ ...f, [k]: v }));
  // Joi validation: serial_cuadro alphanum min(5) max(20), modelo required
  const joiSerieOk = /^[a-zA-Z0-9-]+$/.test(form.serie) && form.serie.length >= 5 && form.serie.length <= 20;
  const joiSerieMsg = !form.serie ? "" : !joiSerieOk
    ? (form.serie.length < 5 ? "Mínimo 5 caracteres" : form.serie.length > 20 ? "Máximo 20 caracteres" : "Solo letras, números y guiones")
    : "";
  const canStep1 = form.marca.trim() && form.modelo.trim() && joiSerieOk;
  const canStep2 = uploads.lateral && uploads.cuadro;

  // nextStep: oculta pasos anteriores, muestra el actual y actualiza dots (React via setStep)
  const nextStep = (n) => {
    setStep(n);
    if (n === 2) showToast("Identificación guardada ✓", "success");
    if (n === 3) showToast("Fotos validadas correctamente ✓", "success");
  };

  // generarNFTRodaid() — 4 pasos: sha256 → subirAIPFS → safeMint → tx.wait()
  const finalizarRegistro = () => {
    setGenerating(true);
    setBfaStep(1);
    showToast("Generando Hash de Seguridad...", "info");
    const chars = "0123456789abcdef";
    const mkHash = (len=40) => "0x" + Array.from({length:len}, () => chars[Math.floor(Math.random()*16)]).join("");
    const mkIpfs = () => "Qm" + Array.from({length:44}, () => "ABCDEFGHJKLMNPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijkmnopqrstuvwxyz123456789"[Math.floor(Math.random()*58)]).join("");

    // Paso 1: ethers.utils.sha256(dataInspeccion)
    let h = "0x", i = 0;
    const iv = setInterval(() => {
      h += chars[Math.floor(Math.random()*16)];
      setHashVal(h + "...");
      i++;
      if (i >= 16) {
        clearInterval(iv);
        setHashVal(mkHash());

        // Paso 2: subirAIPFS(metadata) — IPFS distribuido
        setTimeout(() => {
          setBfaStep(2);
          showToast("Subiendo metadata a IPFS...", "info");
          setIpfsHash(mkIpfs());

          // Paso 3: contract.safeMint(wallet_usuario, ipfsHash)
          setTimeout(() => {
            setBfaStep(3);
            showToast("Auth: Bearer ✓ → safeMint()", "info");

            // Paso 4: tx.wait() — confirmación de red
            setTimeout(() => {
              setBfaStep(4);
              const receipt = mkHash();
              setTxHash(receipt);
              const tid = String(Math.floor(Math.random()*9000)+1000);
              setTokenId(tid);
              setOpenseaUrl(`https://testnets.opensea.io/assets/bfa/${tid}`);
              showToast("Confirmación de red recibida ✓", "success");
              setTimeout(() => {
                setIdRodaid("rodaid_" + mkHash(12).slice(2));
                setGenerating(false);
                setDone(true);
                showToast("¡Certificado emitido con éxito!", "success");
              }, 700);
            }, 1100);
          }, 1100);
        }, 1000);
      }
    }, 55);
  };

  const inputStyle = {
    width:"100%", padding:"12px 14px",
    background:"rgba(255,255,255,.05)", border:`1px solid ${BO}`,
    borderRadius:"10px", color:TX, fontSize:"14px", outline:"none",
    transition:"border-color .2s", fontFamily:"inherit",
  };

  // Step indicator
  const StepDots = () => (
    <div className="step-indicator">
      {[1,2,3].map((s, i) => (
        <div key={s} style={{ display:"contents" }}>
          <div className={`step-dot${step > s ? " done" : step === s ? " active" : ""}`}>
            {step > s ? "✓" : s}
          </div>
          {i < 2 && <div className={`step-line${step > s ? " done" : ""}`} />}
        </div>
      ))}
    </div>
  );

  if (done) return (
    <section style={{ padding:"5rem 2rem", textAlign:"center" }}>
      <div style={{ maxWidth:"520px", margin:"0 auto" }}>
        <div style={{ width:"80px", height:"80px", borderRadius:"50%", background:"rgba(43,188,184,.15)", border:`2px solid ${T}`, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", fontSize:"36px", margin:"0 auto 1.5rem" }}>🎉</div>
        <div style={lbl()}>Certificado generado</div>
        <div style={lbl()}>res.status(201)</div>
        <h2 style={{ ...syne, fontSize:"2rem", fontWeight:800, marginBottom:".5rem", letterSpacing:"-0.5px" }}>¡Bicicleta registrada!</h2>
        <div style={{ background:"rgba(43,188,184,.08)", border:"1px solid rgba(43,188,184,.2)", borderRadius:"10px", padding:".65rem 1rem", marginBottom:"1.25rem", ...mono, fontSize:"12px", textAlign:"left" }}>
          <span style={{ color:MU }}>{"{ "}</span>
          <span style={{ color:T }}>mensaje</span><span style={{ color:MU }}>: </span><span style={{ color:"#a8d8a8" }}>"Certificado Emitido Exitosamente"</span>
          <span style={{ color:MU }}>, </span>
          <span style={{ color:T }}>id_rodaid</span><span style={{ color:MU }}>: </span><span style={{ color:O }}>{idRodaid}</span>
          <span style={{ color:MU }}>{" }"}</span>
        </div>
        <p style={{ color:MU, lineHeight:1.75, marginBottom:"1.25rem" }}>
          <strong style={{color:TX}}>{form.marca} {form.modelo}</strong> anclada en la Blockchain Federal Argentina.
        </p>
        <div style={{ background:"rgba(0,0,0,.25)", border:"1px solid rgba(43,188,184,.3)", borderRadius:"12px", padding:"1rem 1.25rem", marginBottom:".75rem", textAlign:"left" }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize:"10px", color:MU, marginBottom:".35rem", letterSpacing:"1.5px" }}>DATA HASH · SHA-256</div>
          <code style={{ fontSize:"12px", color:T, ...mono, wordBreak:"break-all" }}>{hashVal}</code>
        </div>
        <div style={{ background:"rgba(0,0,0,.2)", border:`1px solid ${BO}`, borderRadius:"12px", padding:".85rem 1.25rem", marginBottom:".75rem", textAlign:"left" }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize:"10px", color:MU, marginBottom:".35rem", letterSpacing:"1.5px" }}>hash_bfa · BFA TRANSACTION</div>
          <code style={{ fontSize:"12px", color:O, ...mono, wordBreak:"break-all" }}>{txHash}</code>
        </div>
        {/* NFT metadata — OpenSea style */}
        <div style={{ background:"rgba(43,188,184,.06)", border:"1px solid rgba(43,188,184,.2)", borderRadius:"12px", padding:".85rem 1.25rem", marginBottom:".75rem", textAlign:"left" }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize:"10px", color:MU, marginBottom:".5rem", letterSpacing:"1.5px" }}>NFT METADATA · ERC-721 · IPFS</div>
          <div style={{ ...mono, fontSize:"11px", lineHeight:1.8 }}>
            <div><span style={{color:MU}}>name: </span><span style={{color:"#a8d8a8"}}>"RODAID CIT - {form.serie}"</span></div>
            <div><span style={{color:MU}}>description: </span><span style={{color:"#a8d8a8"}}>"Certificado de Identidad Técnica · Ley 9556"</span></div>
            <div><span style={{color:MU}}>ipfsHash: </span><span style={{color:T}}>{ipfsHash}</span></div>
            <div><span style={{color:MU}}>tokenId: </span><span style={{color:O}}>#{tokenId}</span></div>
          </div>
        </div>
        {openseaUrl && (
          <div style={{ background:"rgba(244,123,32,.06)", border:"1px solid rgba(244,123,32,.2)", borderRadius:"10px", padding:".65rem 1rem", marginBottom:".75rem", textAlign:"left" }}>
            <div style={{ fontSize:"10px", color:MU, marginBottom:".25rem", letterSpacing:"1.5px" }}>OPENSEA TESTNET URL</div>
            <code style={{ fontSize:"11px", color:O, ...mono, wordBreak:"break-all" }}>{openseaUrl}</code>
          </div>
        )}
        {/* POST /api/cit/aprobar — rodaiEvents.emit('cit_emitido') */}
        <div style={{ background:"rgba(43,188,184,.06)", border:"1px solid rgba(43,188,184,.2)", borderRadius:"10px", padding:".75rem 1rem", marginBottom:".75rem", textAlign:"left" }}>
          <div style={{ ...mono, fontSize:"10px", color:T, marginBottom:".35rem", fontWeight:700 }}>rodaiEvents.emit('cit_emitido')</div>
          <div style={{ fontSize:"12px", color:TX, lineHeight:1.6, marginBottom:".35rem" }}>
            "Tu Certificado de Identidad Técnica (CIT) ha sido emitido con éxito. Ya puedes verlo en tu Wallet."
          </div>
          <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:".4rem", flexWrap:"wrap" }}>
            {[{icon:"📱",l:"Push"},{ icon:"📧",l:"Email → "+form.email}].map((ch,i)=>(
              <span key={i} style={{ fontSize:"10px", fontWeight:600, padding:"2px 8px", borderRadius:"6px", background:"rgba(43,188,184,.12)", color:T, border:"1px solid rgba(43,188,184,.2)" }}>{ch.icon} {ch.l}</span>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
        <div style={{ background:"rgba(0,0,0,.2)", borderRadius:"12px", padding:"1rem 1.25rem", marginBottom:"1.5rem", textAlign:"left" }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize:"10px", color:MU, marginBottom:".5rem", letterSpacing:"1.5px" }}>DATOS DEL CERTIFICADO</div>
          {[["N° Cuadro",form.serie],["Modelo",`${form.marca} ${form.modelo}`],["Puntos técnicos",`${puntosOk}/10`],["resultado_final",resultado_final],["id_rodaid",idRodaid||"rodaid_..."],["NFT","RCIT #" + (tokenId||"?") + " · BFA"],["Red","Mendoza-Mainnet · BFA"]].map(([l,v],i) => (
            <div key={i} style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", fontSize:"13px", padding:".3rem 0", borderBottom:i<3?`1px solid ${BO}`:"none" }}>
              <span style={{ color:MU }}>{l}</span>
              <span style={{ fontWeight:600, fontFamily:l==="N° Cuadro"?"monospace":"inherit" }}>{v}</span>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
        <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:"10px", justifyContent:"center", flexWrap:"wrap" }}>
          <button onClick={() => nav("dashboard")} style={btnP()}>Ver en mi garaje →</button>
          <button onClick={() => { setStep(1); setForm({marca:"",modelo:"",serie:""}); setUploads({lateral:false,cuadro:false,factura:false}); setDone(false); setHashVal(""); setTxHash(""); setBfaStep(0); setPuntos({estructura:false,direccion:false,ergonomia:false,transmision:false,frenado:false,ruedas:false,identidad:false,conservacion:false,mantenimiento:false,inventario:false}); setIdRodaid(""); setIpfsHash(""); setTokenId(""); setOpenseaUrl(""); setBfaStep(0); }} style={btnS()}>Registrar otra</button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>
  );

  return (
    <section style={{ padding:"4rem 2rem" }}>
      <div style={{ maxWidth:"640px", margin:"0 auto" }}>
        <div style={{ textAlign:"center", marginBottom:"2rem" }}>
          <div style={lbl()}>Garaje digital</div>
          <h1 style={{ ...syne, fontSize:"clamp(1.7rem,3vw,2.2rem)", fontWeight:800, letterSpacing:"-0.5px" }}>
            Registrar <span style={{color:O}}>Nueva Unidad</span>
          </h1>
        </div>

        <StepDots />

        {/* Step labels */}
        <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", marginBottom:"2rem", padding:"0 0.5rem" }}>
          {[{s:1,l:"Identificación"},{s:2,l:"Evidencia visual"},{s:3,l:"Confirmación"}].map(({s,l}) => (
            <div key={s} style={{ fontSize:"11px", fontWeight:700, color:step===s?TX:MU, transition:"color .3s", textAlign:"center", flex:1 }}>{l}</div>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* ── PASO 1 ── */}
        {step === 1 && (
          <div className="pa">
            <div style={{ ...card(), marginBottom:"1.5rem" }}>
              <div style={{ ...lbl(T), marginBottom:"1.25rem" }}>Identificación base</div>
              {[
                {k:"marca", l:"Marca", ph:"Ej: Specialized, Trek, Venzo..."},
                {k:"modelo", l:"Modelo y año", ph:"Ej: Rockhopper 2024"},
                {k:"serie", l:"Número de cuadro (serial)", ph:"Ubicado bajo el eje de pedales", hint:"Dato vital para la validez legal del certificado."},
              ].map(f => (
                <div key={f.k} style={{ marginBottom:"1.1rem" }}>
                  <label style={{ fontSize:"12px", fontWeight:700, color:MU, display:"block", marginBottom:".4rem", letterSpacing:".5px" }}>{f.l}</label>
                  <input
                    value={form[f.k]} onChange={e => update(f.k, e.target.value)}
                    placeholder={f.ph} style={inputStyle}
                    onFocus={e => e.target.style.borderColor = T}
                    onBlur={e => e.target.style.borderColor = BO}
                  />
                  {f.k === "serie" && joiSerieMsg && <small style={{ fontSize:"11px", color:"#FF6B6B", marginTop:".3rem", display:"block" }}>⚠ {joiSerieMsg}</small>}
                  {f.k === "serie" && joiSerieOk && form.serie && <small style={{ fontSize:"11px", color:T, marginTop:".3rem", display:"block" }}>✓ Joi: alphanum · min(5) · max(20)</small>}
                  {f.hint && f.k !== "serie" && <small style={{ fontSize:"11px", color:MU, marginTop:".3rem", display:"block" }}>{f.hint}</small>}
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
            <button onClick={() => canStep1 && nextStep(2)} style={{ ...btnP({ width:"100%" }), opacity:canStep1?1:.5 }}>
              Continuar →
            </button>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* ── PASO 2 ── */}
        {step === 2 && (
          <div className="pa">
            <div style={{ ...card(), marginBottom:"1.5rem" }}>
              <div style={{ ...lbl(T), marginBottom:"1.25rem" }}>Pruebas visuales</div>
              <p style={{ fontSize:"13px", color:MU, marginBottom:"1.25rem", lineHeight:1.6 }}>
                Subí fotos que acrediten la posesión de la bicicleta. La foto lateral y del número de cuadro son obligatorias.
              </p>
              <div className="upload-grid" style={{ marginBottom:"1rem" }}>
                {[
                  {k:"lateral", icon:"📸", l:"Foto Lateral", req:true},
                  {k:"cuadro", icon:"🔍", l:"Foto N° Cuadro", req:true},
                  {k:"factura", icon:"📄", l:"Factura", req:false},
                ].map(item => (
                  <div key={item.k}
                    className={`upload-box${uploads[item.k] ? " loaded" : ""}`}
                    onClick={() => setUploads(u => ({ ...u, [item.k]: !u[item.k] }))}>
                    <span>{uploads[item.k] ? "✅" : item.icon}</span>
                    <span className="ulabel">{item.l}</span>
                    <p>{uploads[item.k] ? "Cargado" : item.req ? "Obligatorio" : "Opcional"}</p>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
              {!canStep2 && (
                <div style={{ fontSize:"12px", color:O, background:"rgba(244,123,32,.08)", border:"1px solid rgba(244,123,32,.2)", borderRadius:"8px", padding:".6rem 1rem" }}>
                  ⚠️ Hacé click en las cajas para simular la carga de fotos obligatorias.
                </div>
              )}
              {/* Joi — puntos_tecnicos (10 categorías Boolean) */}
              <div style={{ marginTop:"1rem", background:"rgba(0,0,0,.15)", borderRadius:"12px", padding:"1rem" }}>
                <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"space-between", marginBottom:".75rem", flexWrap:"wrap", gap:".5rem" }}>
                  <div style={{ fontSize:"12px", fontWeight:700, color:T, letterSpacing:".5px" }}>puntos_tecnicos · Joi.object()</div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize:"11px", color:MU }}>{puntosOk}/10 — resultado: <span style={{ color:rfColor, fontWeight:700 }}>{resultado_final}</span></div>
                </div>
                <div style={{ display:"grid", gridTemplateColumns:"repeat(auto-fill,minmax(130px,1fr))", gap:".4rem" }}>
                  {Object.keys(puntos).map(k => (
                    <button key={k} onClick={() => togglePunto(k)} style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:".4rem", padding:".4rem .6rem", borderRadius:"8px", border:`1px solid ${puntos[k] ? "rgba(43,188,184,.4)" : BO}`, background: puntos[k] ? "rgba(43,188,184,.1)" : CB, cursor:"pointer", fontSize:"11px", fontWeight:600, color: puntos[k] ? T : MU, transition:"all .2s", textAlign:"left" }}>
                      <span style={{ width:"14px", height:"14px", borderRadius:"3px", border:`1px solid ${puntos[k] ? T : BO}`, background: puntos[k] ? T : "transparent", display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", fontSize:"9px", color:"white", flexShrink:0 }}>{puntos[k] ? "✓" : ""}</span>
                      {k}
                    </button>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:".75rem" }}>
              <button onClick={() => setStep(1)} style={{ ...btnS({ flex:"1" }) }}>← Atrás</button>
              <button onClick={() => canStep2 && nextStep(3)} style={{ ...btnP({ flex:"2" }), opacity:canStep2?1:.5 }}>Validar datos →</button>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* ── PASO 3 ── */}
        {step === 3 && (
          <div className="pa">
            <div style={{ ...card({ textAlign:"center", padding:"2rem" }), marginBottom:"1.5rem" }}>
              <div style={{ width:"64px", height:"64px", borderRadius:"50%", background:"rgba(43,188,184,.12)", border:`2px solid ${T}`, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", fontSize:"28px", margin:"0 auto 1.25rem", animation:"pulse 2s infinite" }}>⛓️</div>
              <div style={lbl()}>¡Todo listo para certificar!</div>
              <h3 style={{ ...syne, fontSize:"1.4rem", fontWeight:800, marginBottom:".5rem" }}>Confirmación blockchain</h3>
              <div style={{ display:"inline-flex", alignItems:"center", gap:"6px", background:`rgba(${resultado_final==="aprobado"?"43,188,184":resultado_final==="observado"?"244,123,32":"255,107,107"},.12)`, border:`1px solid rgba(${resultado_final==="aprobado"?"43,188,184":resultado_final==="observado"?"244,123,32":"255,107,107"},.3)`, color:rfColor, fontSize:"12px", fontWeight:700, padding:"4px 14px", borderRadius:"20px", marginBottom:"1rem" }}>
                resultado_final: "{resultado_final}"
              </div>
              <p style={{ color:MU, fontSize:"13px", lineHeight:1.75, maxWidth:"380px", margin:"0 auto 1.5rem" }}>
                Al confirmar, se generará un hash SHA-256 único en la Blockchain Federal Argentina vinculado a tu identidad y al número de serie del cuadro.
              </p>

              {/* Resumen */}
              <div style={{ background:"rgba(0,0,0,.2)", borderRadius:"12px", padding:"1rem", marginBottom:"1.25rem", textAlign:"left" }}>
                <div style={{ fontSize:"10px", color:MU, marginBottom:".5rem", letterSpacing:"1.5px" }}>RESUMEN DE REGISTRO</div>
                {[["Marca",form.marca],["Modelo",form.modelo],["N° Cuadro",form.serie]].map(([l,v],i) => (
                  <div key={i} style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", fontSize:"13px", padding:".3rem 0", borderBottom:`1px solid ${BO}` }}>
                    <span style={{ color:MU }}>{l}</span><span style={{ fontWeight:600 }}>{v}</span>
                  </div>
                ))}
                <div style={{ display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", fontSize:"13px", padding:".3rem 0" }}>
                  <span style={{ color:MU }}>Fotos cargadas</span><span style={{ fontWeight:600, color:T }}>{Object.values(uploads).filter(Boolean).length} / 3</span>
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* POST /api/cit/registrar — route pipeline */}
              <div style={{ background:"rgba(0,0,0,.2)", borderRadius:"10px", padding:".75rem 1rem", marginBottom:"1rem", fontSize:"11px", ...mono }}>
                <div style={{ color:MU, marginBottom:".4rem", fontSize:"10px", letterSpacing:"1px" }}>POST /api/cit/registrar</div>
                <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:".25rem", flexWrap:"wrap", justifyContent:"center" }}>
                  {["authMiddleware","validarInspeccion","db.save()","registrarEnBFA()"].map((s,i,a) => (
                    <span key={s} style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", gap:".25rem" }}>
                      <span style={{ background:`rgba(${i<2?"244,123,32":"43,188,184"},.15)`, border:`1px solid rgba(${i<2?"244,123,32":"43,188,184"},.3)`, color: i<2?O:T, padding:"2px 8px", borderRadius:"6px", fontSize:"10px", fontWeight:600 }}>{s}</span>
                      {i<a.length-1 && <span style={{ color:MU }}>→</span>}
                    </span>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* crearPreferenciaPago() — Mercado Pago Split */}
              <div style={{ background:"rgba(0,0,0,.18)", border:`1px solid ${BO}`, borderRadius:"12px", padding:"1rem", marginBottom:"1rem", textAlign:"left" }}>
                <div style={{ fontSize:"10px", color:MU, marginBottom:".6rem", letterSpacing:"1.5px" }}>RODAID PAY · MERCADO PAGO SPLIT</div>
                <div style={{ display:"grid", gridTemplateColumns:"1fr 1fr", gap:".5rem", marginBottom:".6rem" }}>
                  <div style={{ background:"rgba(43,188,184,.08)", borderRadius:"8px", padding:".5rem .75rem" }}>
                    <div style={{ fontSize:"10px", color:MU, marginBottom:"2px" }}>arancelTotal</div>
                    <div style={{ ...syne, fontSize:"15px", fontWeight:800, color:TX }}>$5.000 ARS</div>
                  </div>
                  <div style={{ background:"rgba(244,123,32,.08)", borderRadius:"8px", padding:".5rem .75rem" }}>
                    <div style={{ fontSize:"10px", color:MU, marginBottom:"2px" }}>marketplace_fee · 20%</div>
                    <div style={{ ...syne, fontSize:"15px", fontWeight:800, color:O }}>$1.000 ARS</div>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:".4rem", flexWrap:"wrap", fontSize:"11px", ...mono }}>
                  <span style={{ background:"rgba(43,188,184,.1)", color:T, padding:"3px 8px", borderRadius:"6px" }}>Aliado: $4.000 (80%)</span>
                  <span style={{ background:"rgba(244,123,32,.1)", color:O, padding:"3px 8px", borderRadius:"6px" }}>RODAID: $1.000 (20%)</span>
                  <span style={{ background:"rgba(255,255,255,.05)", color:MU, padding:"3px 8px", borderRadius:"6px" }}>currency_id: ARS</span>
                </div>
                <div style={{ marginTop:".6rem", fontSize:"10px", color:MU, ...mono }}>
                  external_reference: <span style={{ color:T }}>{form.serie||"serial_cuadro"}</span> · notification_url: api.rodaid.com.ar/webhook-pagos
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* Costo */}
              <div style={{ display:"inline-flex", alignItems:"center", gap:"8px", background:"rgba(43,188,184,.12)", border:"1px solid rgba(43,188,184,.3)", color:T, fontSize:"13px", fontWeight:700, padding:"8px 20px", borderRadius:"20px", marginBottom:"1.5rem" }}>
                <span style={{ width:"7px", height:"7px", background:T, borderRadius:"50%", display:"inline-block", animation:"pulse 2s infinite" }} />
                COSTO: 100 PUNTOS · Red BFA
              </div>

              {/* BFA 3-step animation — registrarEnBlockchain() */}
              {generating && (
                <div style={{ background:"rgba(0,0,0,.25)", borderRadius:"12px", padding:"1rem", marginBottom:"1rem", textAlign:"left" }}>
                  {[
                    { step:1, label:"ethers.utils.sha256(dataInspeccion)", desc:"Hash SHA-256 de los datos del CIT" },
                    { step:2, label:"subirAIPFS(metadata)", desc:"Metadata ERC-721 → IPFS distribuido" },
                    { step:3, label:"contract.safeMint(wallet, ipfsHash)", desc:"Acuñando NFT en BFA · Ley 9556" },
                    { step:4, label:"await tx.wait()", desc:"Esperando confirmación de la red" },
                  ].map(s => (
                    <div key={s.step} style={{ display:"flex", gap:".75rem", alignItems:"center", padding:".4rem 0", opacity: bfaStep >= s.step ? 1 : .3, transition:"opacity .4s" }}>
                      <div style={{ width:"20px", height:"20px", borderRadius:"50%", background: bfaStep > s.step ? T : bfaStep === s.step ? O : "rgba(255,255,255,.1)", flexShrink:0, display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"center", fontSize:"10px", fontWeight:700, transition:"background .4s" }}>
                        {bfaStep > s.step ? "✓" : s.step}
                      </div>
                      <div style={{ flex:1 }}>
                        <div style={{ ...mono, fontSize:"11px", color: bfaStep >= s.step ? T : MU }}>{s.label}</div>
                        <div style={{ fontSize:"10px", color:MU }}>{s.desc}</div>
                      </div>
                      {bfaStep === s.step && <div style={{ width:"14px", height:"14px", borderRadius:"50%", border:`2px solid ${O}`, borderTop:"2px solid transparent", animation:"spin 1s linear infinite" }} />}
                    </div>
                  ))}
                  {hashVal && (
                    <div style={{ marginTop:".75rem", padding:".5rem .75rem", background:"rgba(43,188,184,.08)", borderRadius:"8px", ...mono, fontSize:"11px", color:T, wordBreak:"break-all" }}>
                      <span style={{ color:MU }}>dataHash: </span>{hashVal}
                    </div>
                  )}
                  {ipfsHash && (
                    <div style={{ marginTop:".35rem", padding:".5rem .75rem", background:"rgba(244,123,32,.06)", borderRadius:"8px", ...mono, fontSize:"11px", color:O, wordBreak:"break-all" }}>
                      <span style={{ color:MU }}>ipfsHash: </span>{ipfsHash}
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
            <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:".75rem" }}>
              <button onClick={() => setStep(2)} style={{ ...btnS({ flex:"1" }) }} disabled={generating}>← Atrás</button>
              <button onClick={finalizarRegistro} disabled={generating} style={{ ...btnP({ flex:"2", opacity:generating?.6:1 }) }}>
                {generating ? "Generando Hash..." : "GENERAR CERTIFICADO DIGITAL"}
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </section>
  );
}

// ─── MAIN APP ────────────────────────────────────────────
// ─── RODAID-GPT — Agente IA (Claude API) ────────────────
// ─── MODULO STRAVA PREMIUM ───────────────────────────────
function ModuloStravaPremium({ showToast, emitEvent }) {
  const [conectado, setConectado] = useState(false);
  const [conectando, setConectando] = useState(false);
  const [km, setKm] = useState(0);
  const [sincronizando, setSincronizando] = useState(false);

  const iniciarOAuthStrava = () => {
    setConectando(true);
    showToast("Redirigiendo a Strava OAuth...", "info");
    // https://www.strava.com/oauth/authorize?client_id=...&scope=read,activity:read_all
    setTimeout(() => {
      setConectado(true);
      setConectando(false);
      setKm(1247);
      showToast("🧡 Strava conectado · atleta: Federico DG", "success");
    }, 1800);
  };

  const sincronizarKilometraje = async () => {
    setSincronizando(true);
    showToast("Sincronizando métricas desde Strava...", "info");
    // GET /api/v3/athletes/:id/stats · Bearer stravaAccessToken
    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 1600));
    const newKm = km + Math.floor(Math.random() * 80 + 20);
    setKm(newKm);
    setSincronizando(false);
    showToast(`Odómetro actualizado: ${newKm} km`, "success");
    // Alerta mantenimiento preventivo cada ~1000 km
    if (newKm % 1000 < 80) {
      emitEvent("cit_emitido",
        `🚲 Tu bicicleta ha superado un umbral de 1000 km en Strava. Agenda tu revisión de 20 puntos en tu taller aliado de San Martín.`
      );
      showToast("⚙️ Alerta: Revisión de mantenimiento recomendada", "info");
    }
  };

  return (
    <div style={{ ...card({ border:`1px solid rgba(252,76,2,.3)`, background:"#111C2E" }) }}>
      <div style={{ display:"flex", alignItems:"center", justifyContent:"space-between", flexWrap:"wrap", gap:"1rem" }}>
        <div style={{ flex:1 }}>
          <div style={{ display:"inline-block", background:"#FC4C02", color:"white", fontSize:"10px", fontWeight:800, padding:"2px 10px", borderRadius:"10px", letterSpacing:"1px", marginBottom:".5rem" }}>STRAVA INTEGRADO</div>
          <h4 style={{ ...syne, marginTop:".3rem", fontSize:"14px" }}>Sincronización de Rendimiento</h4>
          <p style={{ fontSize:"12px", color:MU, marginTop:".25rem", lineHeight:1.5 }}>
            Vincula tus entrenamientos para automatizar alertas de desgaste y actualizar el historial técnico en BFA.
          </p>
        </div>
        <div>
          {conectado ? (
            <div style={{ display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", alignItems:"flex-end", gap:".5rem" }}>
              <div style={{ color:"#FC4C02", fontWeight:700, fontSize:"13px" }}>🧡 CONECTADO</div>
              <button onClick={sincronizarKilometraje} disabled={sincronizando}
                style={{ fontSize:"11px", fontWeight:600, padding:"6px 14px", borderRadius:"8px", border:`1px solid rgba(252,76,2,.4)`, background:"rgba(252,76,2,.1)", color:"#FC4C02", cursor:"pointer", opacity:sincronizando?.5:1 }}>
                {sincronizando ? "Sincronizando..." : "🔄 Sincronizar"}
              </button>
            </div>
          ) : (
            <button onClick={iniciarOAuthStrava} disabled={conectando}
              style={{ ...btnP({ fontSize:"12px" }), background:"#FC4C02", borderColor:"#FC4C02", opacity:conectando?.6:1 }}>
              {conectando ? "CONECTANDO..." : "CONECTAR STRAVA"}
            </button>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
      {conectado && (
        <div style={{ marginTop:"1rem", paddingTop:"1rem", borderTop:`1px solid ${BO}`, display:"flex", gap:"1.5rem", flexWrap:"wrap" }}>
          <div>
            <div style={{ fontSize:"10px", color:MU, marginBottom:"2px" }}>ODÓMETRO BFA</div>
            <div style={{ ...syne, fontSize:"22px", fontWeight:800, color:"#FC4C02" }}>{km} <span style={{ fontSize:"13px", color:MU }}>km</span></div>
          </div>
          <div>
            <div style={{ fontSize:"10px", color:MU, marginBottom:"2px" }}>PRÓXIMO MANTENIMIENTO</div>
            <div style={{ fontSize:"13px", fontWeight:600, color: (km%1000)<100 ? O : T }}>{1000 - (km%1000)} km restantes</div>
          </div>
          <div style={{ fontSize:"10px", color:MU, ...mono, alignSelf:"flex-end" }}>
            sincronizarKilometrajeBici() · rodaiEvents.emit('MANTENIMIENTO')
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ─── BOTON IMPRESION CIT ──────────────────────────────────
function BotonImpresionCIT({ biciData, onOpenPDF }) {
  const [procesando, setProcesando] = useState(false);
  const ejecutarAccion = async (modo) => {
    setProcesando(true);
    await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 900));
    setProcesando(false);
    if (modo === "descargar") {
      // generarCertificadoPDF() → jsPDF → doc.save(`CIT_RODAID_${serial}.pdf`)
      onOpenPDF && onOpenPDF();
    } else {
      // pdf.autoPrint() → window.open(bloburl,'_blank')
      onOpenPDF && onOpenPDF();
    }
  };
  return (
    <div style={{ ...card({ display:"flex", gap:"1rem", alignItems:"center", flexWrap:"wrap" }) }}>
      <div style={{ flex:1 }}>
        <div style={{ fontSize:"13px", fontWeight:700, marginBottom:"3px" }}>Documentación Legal</div>
        <div style={{ fontSize:"12px", color:MU }}>Descargá o imprimí tu certificado para circular o realizar la compraventa.</div>
      </div>
      <button onClick={() => ejecutarAccion("descargar")} disabled={procesando} style={{ ...btnS({ fontSize:"12px", padding:"8px 16px" }), opacity:procesando?.5:1 }}>
        {procesando ? "..." : "⬇ DESCARGAR PDF"}
      </button>
      <button onClick={() => ejecutarAccion("imprimir")} disabled={procesando} style={{ ...btnP({ fontSize:"12px", padding:"8px 16px" }), opacity:procesando?.5:1 }}>
        {procesando ? "..." : "🖨️ IMPRIMIR"}
      </button>
    </div>
  );
}

function RodaidAIGPT({ showToast }) {
  const [isOpen, setIsOpen] = useState(false);
  const [chat, setChat] = useState([{ role:"ai", text:"¡Hola! Soy Rodaid-GPT 🤖\n\nPuedo ayudarte con:\n• Verificar un serial en la BFA\n• Cotizar tu seguro\n• Informarte sobre el CIT (Ley 9556)\n• Reportar un robo\n\n¿En qué puedo ayudarte?" }]);
  const [input, setInput] = useState("");
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);

  const enviarMensaje = async () => {
    if (!input.trim() || loading) return;
    const userMsg = input.trim();
    setInput("");
    setChat(c => [...c, { role:"user", text:userMsg }]);
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const historial = chat.slice(-6).map(m => ({ role: m.role==="ai"?"assistant":"user", content:m.text }));
      const response = await fetch("https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages", {
        method:"POST",
        headers:{ "Content-Type":"application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          model:"claude-sonnet-4-20250514",
          max_tokens:1000,
          system:`Eres Rodaid-GPT, asistente experto en movilidad segura de Mendoza, Argentina. Ayudas con: verificación de seriales en BFA, certificados CIT (Ley 9556 Mendoza), seguros de bicicleta, alertas de robo, y planes Estándar USD10/mes o Premium USD18/mes (primer mes gratis). RODAID certifica bicis con hash SHA-256 en BFA y emite NFT ERC-721 (RCIT). Responde en español, breve y claro.`,
          messages: [...historial, { role:"user", content:userMsg }],
        })
      });
      const data = await response.json();
      const reply = data.content?.[0]?.text || "No pude procesar tu consulta.";
      setChat(c => [...c, { role:"ai", text:reply }]);
    } catch(e) {
      setChat(c => [...c, { role:"ai", text:"La IA está procesando datos de movilidad, intenta en un momento." }]);
    } finally { setLoading(false); }
  };

  return (
    <div style={{ position:"fixed", bottom:"20px", right:"20px", zIndex:1000 }}>
      {isOpen && (
        <div style={{ width:"340px", height:"440px", display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", background:CB, border:`1px solid ${BO}`, borderRadius:"14px", overflow:"hidden", boxShadow:"0 12px 40px rgba(0,0,0,.6)" }}>
          <div style={{ background:O, padding:"10px 14px", display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"center" }}>
            <span style={{ fontWeight:800, color:"white", fontSize:"14px" }}>🤖 RODAID-GPT</span>
            <button onClick={() => setIsOpen(false)} style={{ color:"white", background:"none", border:"none", cursor:"pointer", fontSize:"16px" }}>✕</button>
          </div>
          <div style={{ flex:1, overflowY:"auto", padding:"12px", display:"flex", flexDirection:"column", gap:"8px" }}>
            {chat.map((m,i) => (
              <div key={i} style={{ alignSelf:m.role==="user"?"flex-end":"flex-start", background:m.role==="user"?O:N, padding:"9px 13px", borderRadius:"12px", fontSize:"13px", maxWidth:"82%", lineHeight:1.55, whiteSpace:"pre-wrap", color:TX }}>{m.text}</div>
            ))}
            {loading && <div style={{ alignSelf:"flex-start", background:N, padding:"9px 13px", borderRadius:"12px", fontSize:"13px", color:MU }}>Analizando...</div>}
          </div>
          <div style={{ padding:"10px", display:"flex", gap:"6px", borderTop:`1px solid ${BO}` }}>
            <input style={{ flex:1, background:N, border:`1px solid ${BO}`, color:TX, padding:"8px 10px", borderRadius:"8px", fontSize:"13px", fontFamily:"inherit", outline:"none" }}
              value={input} onChange={e => setInput(e.target.value)} placeholder="Pregúntame sobre tu bici..."
              onKeyDown={e => e.key==="Enter" && enviarMensaje()} />
            <button onClick={enviarMensaje} disabled={loading} style={{ background:O, border:"none", borderRadius:"8px", padding:"8px 14px", color:"white", cursor:"pointer", fontSize:"14px", opacity:loading?.5:1 }}>➤</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
      {!isOpen && (
        <button onClick={() => setIsOpen(true)} style={{ width:"58px", height:"58px", borderRadius:"50%", background:O, border:"none", cursor:"pointer", boxShadow:`0 4px 20px rgba(244,123,32,.5)`, fontSize:"24px" }}>🤖</button>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

export default function App() {
  const [page, setPage] = useState("inicio");
  const [scrolled, setScrolled] = useState(false);
  const [scrollPct, setScrollPct] = useState(0);
  const [showBackTop, setShowBackTop] = useState(false);
  const [toasts, setToasts] = useState([]);
  // RodaidEvents — class RodaidEvents extends EventEmitter
  const [events, setEvents] = useState([
    { id:1, type:"cit_emitido",        label:"CIT_READY",      msg:"CIT emitido: Trek Marlin 7 · SN-R84MK",        time:"hace 2m",  icon:"🏅", channels:{push:true,  email:true, sms:false} },
    { id:2, type:"oferta_marketplace", label:"NEW_OFFER",       msg:"Nueva oferta en Specialized Rockhopper $380k",  time:"hace 5m",  icon:"🛒", channels:{push:true,  email:true, sms:false} },
    { id:3, type:"alerta_robo",        label:"SECURITY_ALERT",  msg:"⚠️ Alerta: Unidad SN-CGF con denuncia activa", time:"hace 12m", icon:"🚨", channels:{push:true,  email:true, sms:true}  },
  ]);
  const [unread, setUnread] = useState(3);
  const [showNotifs, setShowNotifs] = useState(false);

  // enviarNotificaciones — push always, email always, SMS only SECURITY_ALERT
  const emitEvent = (type, msg) => {
    const icons  = { cit_emitido:"🏅", alerta_robo:"🚨", oferta_marketplace:"🛒", seguro_activado:"🛡️" };
    const labels = { cit_emitido:"CIT_READY", alerta_robo:"SECURITY_ALERT", oferta_marketplace:"NEW_OFFER", seguro_activado:"INSURANCE_ACTIVE" };
    const channels = { push:true, email:true, sms: type==="alerta_robo" };
    setEvents(e => [{ id:Date.now(), type, label:labels[type], msg, time:"ahora", icon:icons[type]||"🔔", channels }, ...e].slice(0,15));
    setUnread(u => u+1);
  };

  const nav = (p) => {
    setPage(p);
    setTimeout(() => window.scrollTo({ top:0, behavior:"smooth" }), 0);
    if (p==="marketplace") emitEvent("oferta_marketplace", "Marketplace visitado — 8 bicis certificadas disponibles");
  };

  const showToast = (msg, type = "success") => {
    // socket.on("notificacion_push") → showToast with mapped type
    const toastType = type === "error" ? "error" : type;
    const id = Date.now();
    setToasts(t => [...t, { id, msg, type: toastType }]);
    setTimeout(() => setToasts(t => t.filter(x => x.id !== id)), 3500);
    // OS Notification API — if Notification.permission === "granted"
    if (typeof Notification !== "undefined" && Notification.permission === "granted") {
      try { new Notification("RODAID Real-Time", { body: msg }); } catch(e) {}
    }
    if (msg.includes("Certificado emitido")) emitEvent("cit_emitido", "Tu Certificado de Identidad Técnica (CIT) ha sido emitido con éxito. Ya puedes verlo en tu Wallet.");
    if (msg.includes("denuncia") || msg.includes("403")) emitEvent("alerta_robo", "⚠️ Unidad con denuncia detectada en verificador");
  };

  // Socket.io — io("https://api.rodaid.com.ar", { auth: { token: userToken } })
  const [socketStatus, setSocketStatus] = useState("connecting");
  const [notifPermission, setNotifPermission] = useState(
    typeof Notification !== "undefined" ? Notification.permission : "default"
  );

  useEffect(() => {
    // Simulate socket connection with auth token
    const connectTimer = setTimeout(() => setSocketStatus("connected"), 1200);
    // Simulate socket.on("notificacion_push") — periodic real-time events
    const pushInterval = setInterval(() => {
      const pushEvents = [
        { mensaje:"Nuevo CIT verificado en la red BFA · Mendoza", tipo:"CIT_READY" },
        { mensaje:"Oferta recibida en tu Specialized Rockhopper", tipo:"NEW_OFFER" },
      ];
      const ev = pushEvents[Math.floor(Math.random()*pushEvents.length)];
      emitEvent(ev.tipo==="NEW_OFFER"?"oferta_marketplace":"cit_emitido", ev.mensaje);
    }, 45000); // every 45s for demo
    return () => { clearTimeout(connectTimer); clearInterval(pushInterval); };
  }, []);

  const requestNotifPermission = () => {
    if (typeof Notification !== "undefined" && Notification.permission === "default") {
      Notification.requestPermission().then(p => setNotifPermission(p));
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    const h = () => {
      const sy = window.scrollY;
      setScrolled(sy > 50);
      setShowBackTop(sy > 400);
      const doc = document.documentElement;
      const pct = (sy / (doc.scrollHeight - doc.clientHeight)) * 100;
      setScrollPct(Math.min(100, pct));
    };
    window.addEventListener("scroll", h, { passive:true });
    return () => window.removeEventListener("scroll", h);
  }, []);

  return (
    <div style={{ background:N, color:TX, minHeight:"100vh", fontFamily:"'Manrope', sans-serif", overflowX:"hidden" }}>
      <style>{GS}</style>
      {/* Scroll progress bar */}
      <div id="scroll-bar" style={{ width:`${scrollPct}%` }} />
      {/* Back to top */}
      {showBackTop && (
        <button id="back-top" onClick={() => window.scrollTo({top:0,behavior:"smooth"})} title="Volver arriba">↑</button>
      )}
      <Navbar p={page} nav={nav} scrolled={scrolled} notifCount={unread} socketStatus={socketStatus} />
      <main className="pa" key={page}>
        {page==="inicio" && <PageInicio nav={nav} showToast={showToast} emitEvent={emitEvent} />}
        {page==="cit" && <PageCIT nav={nav} />}
        {page==="marketplace" && <PageMarketplace nav={nav} emitEvent={emitEvent} />}
        {page==="aliados" && <PageAliados nav={nav} />}
        {page==="planes" && <PagePlanes nav={nav} showToast={showToast} />}
        {page==="terminos" && <PageTerminos nav={nav} />}
        {page==="faq" && <PageFAQ nav={nav} />}
        {page==="registro" && <PageRegistro nav={nav} />}
        {page==="registro-bici" && <PageRegistroBici nav={nav} showToast={showToast} emitEvent={emitEvent} />}
        {page==="verificador" && <PageVerificador nav={nav} showToast={showToast} emitEvent={emitEvent} />}
        {page==="movilidad" && <PageMovilidad nav={nav} showToast={showToast} emitEvent={emitEvent} />}
        {page==="admin-movilidad" && <PageMovilidad nav={nav} showToast={showToast} emitEvent={emitEvent} />}
        {page==="dashboard" && <PageDashboard nav={nav} events={events} emitEvent={emitEvent} showToast={showToast} requestNotifPermission={requestNotifPermission} notifPermission={notifPermission} />}
      </main>
      <RodaidAIGPT showToast={showToast} />
      {showNotifs && (
        <div style={{ position:"fixed", top:"68px", right:"1rem", zIndex:500, background:"#1B2B4B", border:`1px solid ${BO}`, borderRadius:"14px", width:"320px", maxHeight:"400px", overflowY:"auto", boxShadow:"0 16px 48px rgba(0,0,0,.5)" }} onClick={e=>e.stopPropagation()}>
          <div style={{ padding:"1rem 1.25rem", borderBottom:`1px solid ${BO}`, display:"flex", justifyContent:"space-between", alignItems:"center" }}>
            <div style={{ ...syne, fontSize:"13px", fontWeight:700 }}>RodaidEvents</div>
            <div style={{ fontSize:"10px", color:MU, ...mono }}>EventEmitter</div>
          </div>
          {(events||[]).map(ev => (
            <div key={ev.id} style={{ display:"flex", gap:".75rem", padding:".65rem 1.25rem", borderBottom:`1px solid ${BO}`, alignItems:"flex-start" }}>
              <span style={{ fontSize:"16px", flexShrink:0, marginTop:"2px" }}>{ev.icon}</span>
              <div style={{ flex:1, minWidth:0 }}>
                <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:".4rem", alignItems:"center", marginBottom:"2px", flexWrap:"wrap" }}>
                  <span style={{ fontSize:"10px", fontWeight:700, padding:"1px 6px", borderRadius:"4px", background: ev.type==="alerta_robo"?"rgba(255,107,107,.15)":ev.type==="cit_emitido"?"rgba(43,188,184,.15)":"rgba(244,123,32,.15)", color: ev.type==="alerta_robo"?"#FF6B6B":ev.type==="cit_emitido"?T:O }}>{ev.label}</span>
                  <span style={{ fontSize:"10px", color:MU, marginLeft:"auto" }}>{ev.time}</span>
                </div>
                <div style={{ fontSize:"11px", color:TX, lineHeight:1.4, overflow:"hidden", textOverflow:"ellipsis", whiteSpace:"nowrap", marginBottom:"3px" }}>{ev.msg}</div>
                {ev.channels && (
                  <div style={{ display:"flex", gap:".25rem" }}>
                    {[{k:"push",icon:"📱"},{k:"email",icon:"📧"},{k:"sms",icon:"📲"}].map(ch => (
                      <span key={ch.k} style={{ fontSize:"9px", opacity:ev.channels[ch.k]?1:.3 }}>{ch.icon}</span>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
          <div style={{ padding:".75rem 1.25rem", textAlign:"center" }}>
            <div style={{ fontSize:"11px", color:MU, ...mono }}>rodaiEvents.on('cit_emitido' | 'alerta_robo' | 'oferta_marketplace')</div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
      <Footer nav={nav} />
      <Toast toasts={toasts} />
    </div>
  );
}
